I'd like to thank my colleagues @RepAnnaEshoo, @repgregwalden &amp; @FrankPallone for their work &amp; attention on #PAHPA to ensure we are able to keep Americans safe during #publichealth emergencies.
I am proud #PAHPA reflects extensive feedback from the full range of medical &amp; public health preparedness &amp; response stakeholders in order to best examine our response as a nation to threats &amp; to ensure we have clear procedures, resources &amp; support in place to keep Americans safe
Importantly, #PAHPA establishes new advisory groups focused on protecting vulnerable populations such as senior citizens &amp; people w/disabilities during #publichealth threats &amp; emergencies. It also reauthorizes the advisory committee focusing on the specific needs of children.
#PAHPA is a #bipartisan bill that ensures our #healthcare professionals are trained to respond to possible pandemic outbreaks. It prioritizes the further development of our national stockpile of vaccines, basic medical equipment like gloves, hazmat suits &amp; masks, &amp; diagnostics.
In 2001 anthrax attacks infected 17+ people &amp; ended 5 people‚Äôs lives. Since then, the threat of a chemical, biological, radiological or nuclear incident has not dissipated, but instead continues to grow. Our adversaries are continuously looking for ways to produce threats.

"Brooks releases #bipartisan reauthorization bill to protect U.S. from public health threats" &gt;&gt; https://t.co/bxAmx0Vzuj
I'd like to thank @RepAnnaEshoo &amp; my colleagues at @HouseCommerce for their attention to this issue. I cannot emphasize enough how critically important it is to reauthorize #PAHPA before it expires at the end of September.
#PAHPA ensures more #heathcare professionals like nurses/doctors can be hired/trained when facing a #publichealth crisis. It ensures we have a robust supply of vaccines, equipment like gloves, hazmat suits, masks etc in our Strategic National Stockpiles located across the country
To ensure we're better prepared when facing an outbreak like Zika or Ebola, #PAHPA improves the existing Emergency Response Fund so the Secretary doesn't have to wait on approval from Congress to immediately fund the response measures needed to counteract an outbreak &amp; save lives
Our bill reflects extensive feedback from the full range of medical &amp; public health preparedness and response stakeholders. You can see the list here &gt;&gt; https://t.co/xa9lJZSU32
This bipartisan #publichealth &amp; #nationalsecurity effort will ensure our nation is better prepared to respond to natural disasters, emerging infectious diseases, &amp; chemical, biological, radiological or nuclear attacks whether from terrorist groups or from nation states.

The #JakeLairdAct provides grants to encourage states to adopt laws, that require both due process &amp; probable cause, enabling local #lawenforcement to seize &amp; retain firearms from individuals who are determined to be a danger to themselves or others &gt;&gt; https://t.co/WRgyItdQUJ
The families of the victims killed in the tragedy in Parkland, Florida on February 14, 2018, wrote a letter to show their support for the #JakeLairdAct. Read their letter here &gt;&gt; https://t.co/hzSeQPggtU https://t.co/FDgG9mFo0c
The #JakeLairdAct as been used 600+ times in Indy since 2005 &amp; should be used as a model for states nationwide. It enables local law enforcement, w/probable cause, to seize &amp; retain firearms from individuals who are determined to be an imminent danger to themselves or others.
The Jake Laird Act is named after an Indianapolis police officer who was shot &amp; killed in 2004 in the line of duty by a man who struggled with mental illness. This bill provides grants to encourage states to adopt laws, similar to Indiana‚Äôs 2005 Jake Laird Law.
As our country continues to grapple w/how to keep our communities safe, the Jake Laird Act will provide our local law enforcement officers the tools &amp; training necessary to prevent senseless acts of violence from claiming more innocent lives.

Poison control centers save countless lives, prevent toxic exposure &amp; poisoning injury, and reduce billions of dollars in unnecessary #healthcare costs. The data poison centers collect can even be used to identify hotspots for opioid misuse &amp; overdose.
In one month alone, there were 9,039 #opioid exposures reported to poison control centers nationwide.
Since 2011, poison control centers have been working #behindthescenes to fight against the #opioidepidemic &amp; have handled about 500,000 cases of opioid misuse &amp; abuse ‚Äì that‚Äôs approximately 192 cases per day, every day.

Willard's statue is displayed in the @uscapitol. She's remembered for her contributions to women's higher #education &amp; suffrage
In 1888, Frances Willard was one of the founders of the National Council of Women &amp; became its 1st president #WomensHistoryMonth https://t.co/QhwAhGQAsp
She co-founded the Rosa L. Parks Scholarship Foundation in 1980 &amp; the Rosa and Raymond Parks Institute for Self-Development in 1987.
Later, she served as secretary &amp; receptionist to Rep. John Conyers until her retirement in 1988.
She was arrested &amp; found guilty of disorderly conduct and violating a local ordinance for her act of defiance. #WomensHistoryMonth
It honors her famous refusal in 1955 to obey the driver's direction to move from her seat on the bus to make room for a white passenger.
The Rosa Parks statue: 1st full-length statue of an African American person in the @uscapitol &amp; was authorized by Congress in 2005 #WHM2017
Rosa Parks remained an icon of the #civilrights movement until her death. In 1999, Congress honored her with a Congressional Gold Medal.
